gop.matd1.uty -gop.matd1.ntz*gop.matd1.u0x+gop.matd1.ntx*gop.matd1.u0z 1 Tangent to refracted wavefront, y component Rays

gop.matd1.ddelta arg((env_out(real(gop.nref_local))*cos(gop.matd1.thetai)-env_in(real(gop.nref_local))*cos(gop.matd1.thetat))/(env_out(real(gop.nref_local))*cos(gop.matd1.thetai)+env_in(real(gop.nref_local))*cos(gop.matd1.thetat)))-arg((env_in(real(gop.nref_local))*cos(gop.matd1.thetai)-env_out(real(gop.nref_local))*cos(gop.matd1.thetat))/(env_in(real(gop.nref_local))*cos(gop.matd1.thetai)+env_out(real(gop.nref_local))*cos(gop.matd1.thetat))) rad Phase shift Rays

gop.matd1.ts 2*env_in(real(gop.nref_local))*cos(gop.matd1.thetai)/(env_in(real(gop.nref_local))*cos(gop.matd1.thetai)+env_out(real(gop.nref_local))*cos(gop.matd1.thetat)) 1 Transmission coefficient, s-polarized Rays
gop.matd1.rp (env_out(real(gop.nref_local))*cos(gop.matd1.thetai)-env_in(real(gop.nref_local))*cos(gop.matd1.thetat))/(env_out(real(gop.nref_local))*cos(gop.matd1.thetai)+env_in(real(gop.nref_local))*cos(gop.matd1.thetat)) 1 Reflection coefficient, p-polarized Rays
gop.matd1.rs (env_in(real(gop.nref_local))*cos(gop.matd1.thetai)-env_out(real(gop.nref_local))*cos(gop.matd1.thetat))/(env_in(real(gop.nref_local))*cos(gop.matd1.thetai)+env_out(real(gop.nref_local))*cos(gop.matd1.thetat)) 1 Reflection coefficient, s-polarized Rays
gop.matd1.snir1 gop.sn1*cos(2*gop.matd1.thetapi)+gop.sn2*sin(2*gop.matd1.thetapi) 1 Incident normalized stokes parameter 1, rotated Rays
gop.matd1.snir2 -gop.sn1*sin(2*gop.matd1.thetapi)+gop.sn2*cos(2*gop.matd1.thetapi) 1 Incident normalized stokes parameter 2, rotated Rays
gop.matd1.snir3 gop.sn3 1 Incident normalized stokes parameter 3, rotated Rays
gop.matd1.I0t 0.5*gop.I*((1+gop.matd1.snir1)*abs(gop.matd1.ts)^2+(1-gop.matd1.snir1)*abs(gop.matd1.tp)^2)*env_out(gop.nref_local)*cos(gop.matd1.thetat)/(env_in(gop.nref_local)*cos(gop.matd1.thetai)) W/m² Initial intensity, refracted Rays
